<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-logging-cantonfilterevaluator"></a>

## `CantonFilterEvaluator`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/logging/CantonFilterEvaluator.html)

**Signature**

```text
class CantonFilterEvaluator extends EvaluatorFilter[ILoggingEvent]
```

**Summary**

Filters out any events with log level strictly lower than "LOG_LEVEL_CANTON" and logger name starting with "com.daml" or "com.digitalasset". The property "LOG_LEVEL_CANTON" is first read from java system properties, then from the shell environment and then the default of INFO is taken. (This is consistent with the standard logback behavior.)

**Members**

| Docs | Member | Introduced | Deprecated | Removed |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/logging/CantonFilterEvaluator.html#start():Unit) | `start(): Unit` | `3.4.10` | - | - |

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-logging-errorloggingcontext"></a>

## `ErrorLoggingContext`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/logging/ErrorLoggingContext.html)

**Signature**

```text
trait ErrorLoggingContext extends BaseErrorLogger
```

**Summary**

Enriches a com.digitalasset.canton.tracing.TraceContext with a fixed logger and a set of properties. Use this class as an implicit parameter of methods inside helper classes whose class name shall not show up in the log line as part of the logger name. Instead, the logger name and properties are fixed when this object is created, which typically happens at a call site further up via NamedLogging.errorLoggingContext.

## `LastErrorsAppender`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/logging/LastErrorsAppender.html)

**Signature**

```text
class LastErrorsAppender extends AppenderBase[ILoggingEvent] with AppenderAttachable[ILoggingEvent]
```

**Summary**

Logback appender that keeps a bounded queue of errors/warnings that have been logged and associated log entries with the same trace-id.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-logging-namedloggerfactory"></a>

## `NamedLoggerFactory`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/logging/NamedLoggerFactory.html)

**Signature**

```text
trait NamedLoggerFactory extends AnyRef
```

**Summary**

NamedLoggerFactory augments a regular class-based slf4j logger with one annotated with a "name" where the name provides human readable context identifying a class instance, e.g. which participant in a set of participants has logged a particular message.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-logging-namedloggingcontext"></a>

## `NamedLoggingContext`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/logging/NamedLoggingContext.html)

**Signature**

```text
final case class NamedLoggingContext(loggerFactory: NamedLoggerFactory, traceContext: TraceContext) extends Product with Serializable
```

**Summary**

Enriches a com.digitalasset.canton.tracing.TraceContext with a NamedLoggerFactory. This allows to pass a NamedLoggerFactory into methods that themselves do not have a NamedLoggerFactory in scope on their own, e.g., because they live inside a static object or in pure data classes.

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

| [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/logging/NamedLoggingContext.html#debug(message:String,throwable:Throwable)(implicitloggerNameFromClass:com.digitalasset.canton.logging.LoggerNameFromClass):Unit) | `debug(message: String, throwable: Throwable)(loggerNameFromClass: LoggerNameFromClass): Unit` | `3.4.10` | - | - |

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-logging-throttlefilterevaluator"></a>

## `ThrottleFilterEvaluator`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/logging/ThrottleFilterEvaluator.html)

**Signature**

```text
class ThrottleFilterEvaluator extends EvaluatorFilter[ILoggingEvent]
```

**Summary**

Throttles logging events, so that no more than maxLoggedOverPeriod unique events are logged over expiryPeriod. De-duplicates logging events over expiryPeriod. Used to ensure that the interactive console remains usable even when the system is in a bad state and logging many errors. Inspired by https://github.com/RotterdamLogisticsLab/logback-throttle/blob/master/src/main/kotlin/com/portofrotterdam/dbs/public/logback/throttle/Throttle.kt

**Members**

| Docs | Member | Introduced | Deprecated | Removed |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/logging/ThrottleFilterEvaluator.html#expiryPeriod:java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicLong) | `expiryPeriod: AtomicLong` | `3.4.10` | - | - |
| [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/logging/ThrottleFilterEvaluator.html#maxLoggedOverPeriod:java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicLong) | `maxLoggedOverPeriod: AtomicLong` | `3.4.10` | - | - |
| [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/logging/ThrottleFilterEvaluator.html#messageCache:scala.collection.concurrent.TrieMap[String,Long]) | `messageCache: TrieMap[String, Long]` | `3.4.10` | - | - |
| [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/logging/ThrottleFilterEvaluator.html#setExpiryPeriod(newValue:Long):Unit) | `setExpiryPeriod(newValue: Long): Unit` | `3.4.10` | - | - |
| [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/logging/ThrottleFilterEvaluator.html#setMaxLoggedOverPeriod(newValue:Long):Unit) | `setMaxLoggedOverPeriod(newValue: Long): Unit` | `3.4.10` | - | - |
